h1. Pinterest REST API

Pinterest's REST API

*Version:* 5.3.0

----

{expand:Table of Contents - Click to expand}
{toc:printable=true|style=square|minLevel=2|maxLevel=3|type=list|outline=false|include=.*}
{expand}

h2. Endpoints


h3. adAccount/analytics
{panel:title=adAccount/analytics|borderStyle=solid|borderColor=#003b6f|titleBGColor=#003b6f|titleColor=#a6b8c7|bgColor=#ffffff}
    *Summary:* Get ad account analytics
    *Description:* Get analytics for the specified &lt;code&gt;ad_account_id&lt;/code&gt;, filtered by the specified options.
- The token&#39;s user_account must either be the Owner of the specified ad account, or have one of the necessary roles granted to them via &lt;a href&#x3D;&quot;https://help.pinterest.com/en/business/article/share-and-manage-access-to-your-ad-accounts&quot;&gt;Business Access&lt;/a&gt;: Admin, Analyst, Campaign Manager.

	|| HttpMethod | {status:colour=Yellow|title=get|subtle=false} |
    || Protocol | {noformat:nopanel=true}https{noformat} |
    || Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}/ad_accounts/{ad_account_id}/analytics{noformat} |
    || Base Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}https://api.pinterest.com/v5{noformat} |
    || Produces | {noformat:nopanel=true}application/json{noformat} |
----
h4. Parameters
h5. Path Parameters
        ||Name||Description||Type||Required||Default||Pattern||Enum||
        |ad_account_id |Unique identifier of an ad account. | String | (/) |null | /^\d+$/ |  |



h5. Query Parameters
        ||Name||Description||Required||Default||Pattern||
        |start_date |Metric report start date (UTC). Format: YYYY-MM-DD | date | (/) |null |  |  ||end_date |Metric report end date (UTC). Format: YYYY-MM-DD | date | (/) |null |  |  ||columns |Columns to retrieve. **NOTE**: Any metrics defined as MICRO_DOLLARS returns a value based on the advertiser profile&#39;s currency field. For USD,($1/1,000,000, or $0.000001 - one one-ten-thousandth of a cent). it&#39;s microdollars. Otherwise, it&#39;s in microunits of the advertiser&#39;s currency.&lt;br/&gt;For example, if the advertiser&#39;s currency is GBP (British pound sterling), all MICRO_DOLLARS fields will be in GBP microunits (1/1,000,000 British pound).&lt;br/&gt;If a column has no value, it may not be returned | array[String] | (/) |null |  |  ||granularity |Granularity | Granularity | (/) |null |  |  ||click_window_days |Number of days to use as the conversion attribution window for a pin click action. Applies to Pinterest Tag conversion metrics. Prior conversion tags use their defined attribution windows. If not specified, defaults to &#x60;30&#x60; days. | Integer | (x) |30 |  | [1, 7, 30, 60] ||engagement_window_days |Number of days to use as the conversion attribution window for an engagement action. Engagements include saves, closeups, link clicks, and carousel card swipes. Applies to Pinterest Tag conversion metrics. Prior conversion tags use their defined attribution windows. If not specified, defaults to &#x60;30&#x60; days. | Integer | (x) |30 |  | [1, 7, 30, 60] ||view_window_days |Number of days to use as the conversion attribution window for a view action. Applies to Pinterest Tag conversion metrics. Prior conversion tags use their defined attribution windows. If not specified, defaults to &#x60;1&#x60; day. | Integer | (x) |1 |  | [1, 7, 30, 60] ||conversion_report_time |The date by which the conversion metrics returned from this endpoint will be reported. There are two dates associated with a conversion event: the date that the user interacted with the ad, and the date that the user completed a conversion event. | String | (x) |TIME_OF_AD_ACTION |  | [TIME_OF_AD_ACTION, TIME_OF_CONVERSION] |
----
h4. Responses

    	|| Status Code | {status:colour=Green|title=200|subtle=false} |
    	|| Message | Success |
    	|| Response Type | array[map[String, Object]] |
    	|| Response Model | [array[map[String, Object]] Model|#array[map[String, Object]]ModelAnchor|Jump to model] |
    	|| Response Schema | {code:collapse=true}{
  "description" : "Success",
  "content" : {
    "application/json" : {
      "schema" : {
        "$ref" : "#/components/schemas/AdAccountAnalyticsResponse"
      }
    }
  }
}{code} |
       


    	|| Status Code | {status:colour=Green|title=400|subtle=false} |
    	|| Message | Invalid ad account analytics parameters. |
    	|| Response Type | Error |
    	|| Response Model | [Error Model|#ErrorModelAnchor|Jump to model] |
    	|| Response Schema | {code:collapse=true}{
  "description" : "Invalid ad account analytics parameters.",
  "content" : {
    "application/json" : {
      "schema" : {
        "$ref" : "#/components/schemas/Error"
      },
      "example" : {
        "code" : 400,
        "message" : "Invalid ad account analytics parameters."
      }
    }
  }
}{code} |
       


    	|| Status Code | {status:colour=Green|title=0|subtle=false} |
    	|| Message | Unexpected error |
    	|| Response Type | Error |
    	|| Response Model | [Error Model|#ErrorModelAnchor|Jump to model] |
    	|| Response Schema | {code:collapse=true}{
  "description" : "Unexpected error",
  "content" : {
    "application/json" : {
      "schema" : {
        "$ref" : "#/components/schemas/Error"
      }
    }
  }
}{code} |
       

{panel}



h3. adAccounts/list
{panel:title=adAccounts/list|borderStyle=solid|borderColor=#003b6f|titleBGColor=#003b6f|titleColor=#a6b8c7|bgColor=#ffffff}
    *Summary:* List ad accounts
    *Description:* Get a list of the ad_accounts that the &quot;operation user_account&quot; has access to.
- This includes ad_accounts they own and ad_accounts that are owned by others who have granted them &lt;a href&#x3D;&quot;https://help.pinterest.com/en/business/article/share-and-manage-access-to-your-ad-accounts&quot;&gt;Business Access&lt;/a&gt;.

	|| HttpMethod | {status:colour=Yellow|title=get|subtle=false} |
    || Protocol | {noformat:nopanel=true}https{noformat} |
    || Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}/ad_accounts{noformat} |
    || Base Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}https://api.pinterest.com/v5{noformat} |
    || Produces | {noformat:nopanel=true}application/json{noformat} |
----
h4. Parameters



h5. Query Parameters
        ||Name||Description||Required||Default||Pattern||
        |bookmark |Cursor used to fetch the next page of items | String | (x) |null |  |  ||page_size |Maximum number of items to include in a single page of the response. See documentation on &lt;a href&#x3D;&#39;/docs/api/v5/#tag/Pagination&#39;&gt;Pagination&lt;/a&gt; for more information. | Integer | (x) |25 |  |  ||include_shared_accounts |Include shared ad accounts | Boolean | (x) |true |  |  |
----
h4. Responses

    	|| Status Code | {status:colour=Green|title=200|subtle=false} |
    	|| Message | response |
    	|| Response Type | Paginated |
    	|| Response Model | [Paginated Model|#PaginatedModelAnchor|Jump to model] |
    	|| Response Schema | {code:collapse=true}{
  "description" : "response",
  "content" : {
    "application/json" : {
      "schema" : {
        "allOf" : [ {
          "$ref" : "#/components/schemas/Paginated"
        }, {
          "properties" : {
            "items" : {
              "type" : "array",
              "description" : "Ad accounts",
              "items" : {
                "$ref" : "#/components/schemas/AdAccount"
              }
            }
          }
        } ]
      }
    }
  }
}{code} |
       


    	|| Status Code | {status:colour=Green|title=0|subtle=false} |
    	|| Message | Unexpected error |
    	|| Response Type | Error |
    	|| Response Model | [Error Model|#ErrorModelAnchor|Jump to model] |
    	|| Response Schema | {code:collapse=true}{
  "description" : "Unexpected error",
  "content" : {
    "application/json" : {
      "schema" : {
        "$ref" : "#/components/schemas/Error"
      }
    }
  }
}{code} |

h3. adGroups/analytics
{panel:title=adGroups/analytics|borderStyle=solid|borderColor=#003b6f|titleBGColor=#003b6f|titleColor=#a6b8c7|bgColor=#ffffff}
    *Summary:* Get ad group analytics
    *Description:* Get analytics for the specified ad groups in the specified &lt;code&gt;ad_account_id&lt;/code&gt;, filtered by the specified options.
- The token&#39;s user_account must either be the Owner of the specified ad account, or have one of the necessary roles granted to them via &lt;a href&#x3D;&quot;https://help.pinterest.com/en/business/article/share-and-manage-access-to-your-ad-accounts&quot;&gt;Business Access&lt;/a&gt;: Admin, Analyst, Campaign Manager.

	|| HttpMethod | {status:colour=Yellow|title=get|subtle=false} |
    || Protocol | {noformat:nopanel=true}https{noformat} |
    || Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}/ad_accounts/{ad_account_id}/ad_groups/analytics{noformat} |
    || Base Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}https://api.pinterest.com/v5{noformat} |
    || Produces | {noformat:nopanel=true}application/json{noformat} |
----
h4. Parameters
h5. Path Parameters
        ||Name||Description||Type||Required||Default||Pattern||Enum||
        |ad_account_id |Unique identifier of an ad account. | String | (/) |null | /^\d+$/ |  |



h5. Query Parameters
        ||Name||Description||Required||Default||Pattern||
        |start_date |Metric report start date (UTC). Format: YYYY-MM-DD | date | (/) |null |  |  ||end_date |Metric report end date (UTC). Format: YYYY-MM-DD | date | (/) |null |  |  ||ad_group_ids |List of Ad group Ids to use to filter the results. | array[String] | (/) |null |  |  ||columns |Columns to retrieve. **NOTE**: Any metrics defined as MICRO_DOLLARS returns a value based on the advertiser profile&#39;s currency field. For USD,($1/1,000,000, or $0.000001 - one one-ten-thousandth of a cent). it&#39;s microdollars. Otherwise, it&#39;s in microunits of the advertiser&#39;s currency.&lt;br/&gt;For example, if the advertiser&#39;s currency is GBP (British pound sterling), all MICRO_DOLLARS fields will be in GBP microunits (1/1,000,000 British pound).&lt;br/&gt;If a column has no value, it may not be returned | array[String] | (/) |null |  |  ||granularity |Granularity | Granularity | (/) |null |  |  ||click_window_days |Number of days to use as the conversion attribution window for a pin click action. Applies to Pinterest Tag conversion metrics. Prior conversion tags use their defined attribution windows. If not specified, defaults to &#x60;30&#x60; days. | Integer | (x) |30 |  | [1, 7, 30, 60] ||engagement_window_days |Number of days to use as the conversion attribution window for an engagement action. Engagements include saves, closeups, link clicks, and carousel card swipes. Applies to Pinterest Tag conversion metrics. Prior conversion tags use their defined attribution windows. If not specified, defaults to &#x60;30&#x60; days. | Integer | (x) |30 |  | [1, 7, 30, 60] ||view_window_days |Number of days to use as the conversion attribution window for a view action. Applies to Pinterest Tag conversion metrics. Prior conversion tags use their defined attribution windows. If not specified, defaults to &#x60;1&#x60; day. | Integer | (x) |1 |  | [1, 7, 30, 60] ||conversion_report_time |The date by which the conversion metrics returned from this endpoint will be reported. There are two dates associated with a conversion event: the date that the user interacted with the ad, and the date that the user completed a conversion event. | String | (x) |TIME_OF_AD_ACTION |  | [TIME_OF_AD_ACTION, TIME_OF_CONVERSION] |
----
h4. Responses

    	|| Status Code | {status:colour=Green|title=200|subtle=false} |

      "schema" : {
        "$ref" : "#/components/schemas/AdGroupsAnalyticsResponse"

h3. adGroups/list
{panel:title=adGroups/list|borderStyle=solid|borderColor=#003b6f|titleBGColor=#003b6f|titleColor=#a6b8c7|bgColor=#ffffff}
    *Summary:* List ad groups
    *Description:* Get a list of the ad groups in the specified &lt;code&gt;ad_account_id&lt;/code&gt;, filtered by the specified options.
- The token&#39;s user_account must either be the Owner of the specified ad account, or have one of the necessary roles granted to them via &lt;a href&#x3D;&quot;https://help.pinterest.com/en/business/article/share-and-manage-access-to-your-ad-accounts&quot;&gt;Business Access&lt;/a&gt;: Admin, Analyst, Campaign Manager.

	|| HttpMethod | {status:colour=Yellow|title=get|subtle=false} |
    || Protocol | {noformat:nopanel=true}https{noformat} |
    || Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}/ad_accounts/{ad_account_id}/ad_groups{noformat} |
    || Base Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}https://api.pinterest.com/v5{noformat} |
    || Produces | {noformat:nopanel=true}application/json{noformat} |
----
h4. Parameters
h5. Path Parameters
        ||Name||Description||Type||Required||Default||Pattern||Enum||
        |ad_account_id |Unique identifier of an ad account. | String | (/) |null | /^\d+$/ |  |



h5. Query Parameters
        ||Name||Description||Required||Default||Pattern||
        |campaign_ids |List of Campaign Ids to use to filter the results. | array[String] | (x) |null |  |  ||ad_group_ids |List of Ad group Ids to use to filter the results. | array[String] | (x) |null |  |  ||entity_statuses |Entity status | array[String] | (x) |null |  |  ||page_size |Maximum number of items to include in a single page of the response. See documentation on &lt;a href&#x3D;&#39;/docs/api/v5/#tag/Pagination&#39;&gt;Pagination&lt;/a&gt; for more information. | Integer | (x) |25 |  |  ||order |The order in which to sort the items returned: “ASCENDING” or “DESCENDING”
by ID. Note that higher-value IDs are associated with more-recently added
items. | String | (x) |null |  | [ASCENDING, DESCENDING] ||bookmark |Cursor used to fetch the next page of items | String | (x) |null |  |  ||translate_interests_to_names |Return interests as text names (if value is true) rather than topic IDs. | Boolean | (x) |false |  |  |
----

    	|| Status Code | {status:colour=Green|title=200|subtle=false} |

        }, {
          "properties" : {
            "items" : {
              "type" : "array",
              "items" : {
                "$ref" : "#/components/schemas/AdGroupResponse"
              }
            }
          }
        } ]
      }
    }
  }
}{code} |
       


    	|| Status Code | {status:colour=Green|title=400|subtle=false} |
    	|| Message | Invalid ad account group parameters. |

    	|| Response Model | [Error Model|#ErrorModelAnchor|Jump to model] |

    || Produces | {noformat:nopanel=true}application/json{noformat} |

h3. media/create
{panel:title=media/create|borderStyle=solid|borderColor=#003b6f|titleBGColor=#003b6f|titleColor=#a6b8c7|bgColor=#ffffff}
    *Summary:* Register media upload
    *Description:* Register your intent to upload media

The response includes all of the information needed to upload the media
to Pinterest.

To upload the media, make an HTTP POST request (using &lt;tt&gt;curl&lt;/tt&gt;, for
example) to &lt;tt&gt;upload_url&lt;/tt&gt; using the &lt;tt&gt;Content-Type&lt;/tt&gt; header
value. Send the media file&#39;s contents as the request&#39;s &lt;tt&gt;file&lt;/tt&gt;
parameter and also include all of the parameters from
&lt;tt&gt;upload_parameters&lt;/tt&gt;.

&lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href&#x3D;&#39;/docs/solutions/content-apps/#creatingvideopins&#39;&gt;Learn more&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; about video Pin creation.

	|| HttpMethod | {status:colour=Yellow|title=post|subtle=false} |
    || Protocol | {noformat:nopanel=true}https{noformat} |
    || Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}/media{noformat} |
    || Base Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}https://api.pinterest.com/v5{noformat} |

{panel:title=pins/analytics|borderStyle=solid|borderColor=#003b6f|titleBGColor=#003b6f|titleColor=#a6b8c7|bgColor=#ffffff}
    *Summary:* Get Pin analytics
    *Description:* Get analytics for a Pin owned by the &quot;operation user_account&quot; - or on a group board that has been shared with this account.
- By default, the &quot;operation user_account&quot; is the token user_account.

Optional: Business Access: Specify an &lt;code&gt;ad_account_id&lt;/code&gt; (obtained via &lt;a href&#x3D;&quot;https://developers.pinterest.com/docs/api/v5/#operation/ad_accounts/list&quot;&gt;List ad accounts&lt;/a&gt;) to use the owner of that ad_account as the &quot;operation user_account&quot;. In order to do this, the token user_account must have one of the following &lt;a href&#x3D;&quot;https://help.pinterest.com/en/business/article/share-and-manage-access-to-your-ad-accounts&quot;&gt;Business Access&lt;/a&gt; roles on the ad_account:

- For Pins on public or protected boards: Admin, Analyst.
- For Pins on secret boards: Admin.

h3. pins/create
{panel:title=pins/create|borderStyle=solid|borderColor=#003b6f|titleBGColor=#003b6f|titleColor=#a6b8c7|bgColor=#ffffff}
    *Summary:* Create Pin
    *Description:* Create a Pin on a board or board section owned by the &quot;operation user_account&quot;.

Note: If the current &quot;operation user_account&quot; (defined by the access token) has access to another user&#39;s Ad Accounts via Pinterest Business Access, you can modify your request to make use of the current operation_user_account&#39;s permissions to those Ad Accounts by including the ad_account_id in the path parameters for the request (e.g. .../?ad_account_id&#x3D;12345&amp;...).

- This function is intended solely for publishing new content created by the user. If you are interested in saving content created by others to your Pinterest boards, sometimes called &#39;curated content&#39;, please use our &lt;a href&#x3D;&#39;/docs/add-ons/save-button&#39;&gt;Save button&lt;/a&gt; instead. For more tips on creating fresh content for Pinterest, review our &lt;a href&#x3D;&#39;/docs/solutions/content-apps&#39;&gt;Content App Solutions Guide&lt;/a&gt;.

&lt;strong&gt;&lt;a href&#x3D;&#39;/docs/solutions/content-apps/#creatingvideopins&#39;&gt;Learn more&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; about video Pin creation.

    *Summary:* Get Pin
    *Description:* Get a Pin owned by the &quot;operation user_account&quot; - or on a group board that has been shared with this account.
- By default, the &quot;operation user_account&quot; is the token user_account.

Optional: Business Access: Specify an &lt;code&gt;ad_account_id&lt;/code&gt; (obtained via &lt;a href&#x3D;&#39;/docs/api/v5/#operation/ad_accounts/list&#39;&gt;List ad accounts&lt;/a&gt;) to use the owner of that ad_account as the &quot;operation user_account&quot;. - For Pins on public or protected boards: Owner, Admin, Analyst, Campaign Manager.
- For Pins on secret boards: Owner, Admin.

	|| HttpMethod | {status:colour=Yellow|title=get|subtle=false} |
    || Protocol | {noformat:nopanel=true}https{noformat} |
    || Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}/pins/{pin_id}{noformat} |
    || Base Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}https://api.pinterest.com/v5{noformat} |
    || Produces | {noformat:nopanel=true}application/json{noformat} |

h4. Parameters
h5. Path Parameters
        ||Name||Description||Type||Required||Default||Pattern||Enum||
        |pin_id |Unique identifier of a Pin. | String | (/) |null |  |  |



h5. Query Parameters
        ||Name||Description||Required||Default||Pattern||

h3. userAccount/analytics
{panel:title=userAccount/analytics|borderStyle=solid|borderColor=#003b6f|titleBGColor=#003b6f|titleColor=#a6b8c7|bgColor=#ffffff}
    *Summary:* Get user account analytics
    *Description:* Get analytics for the &quot;operation user_account&quot;
- By default, the &quot;operation user_account&quot; is the token user_account.

Optional: Business Access: Specify an ad_account_id to use the owner of that ad_account as the &quot;operation user_account&quot;.

	|| HttpMethod | {status:colour=Yellow|title=get|subtle=false} |
    || Protocol | {noformat:nopanel=true}https{noformat} |
    || Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}/user_account/analytics{noformat} |
    || Base Path | {noformat:nopanel=true}https://api.pinterest.com/v5{noformat} |
    || Produces | {noformat:nopanel=true}application/json{noformat} |
----
h4. Parameters

        ||Name||Description||Required||Default||Pattern||
        |start_date |Metric report start date (UTC). Format: YYYY-MM-DD | date | (/) |null |  |  ||end_date |Metric report end date (UTC). Format: YYYY-MM-DD | date | (/) |null |  |  ||from_claimed_content |Filter on Pins that match your claimed domain. | String | (x) |BOTH |  | [OTHER, CLAIMED, BOTH] ||pin_format |Pin formats to get data for, default is all. | String | (x) |ALL |  | [ALL, PRODUCT, REGULAR, VIDEO] ||app_types |Apps or devices to get data for, default is all. | String | (x) |ALL |  | [ALL, MOBILE, TABLET, WEB] ||metric_types |Metric types to get data for, default is all.  | array[String] | (x) |null |  |  ||split_field |How to split the data into groups. Not including this param means data won&#39;t be split. | String | (x) |NO_SPLIT |  | [NO_SPLIT, APP_TYPE, OWNED_CONTENT, PIN_FORMAT] ||ad_account_id |Unique identifier of an ad account. | String | (x) |null | /^\d+$/ |  |

        {anchor:TrackingUrlsModelAnchor}
        h3. TrackingUrls

        Third-party tracking URLs. Up to three tracking URLs are supported for each event type. Tracking URLs set at the ad group or ad level can override those set at the campaign level. For more information, see <a href="https://help.pinterest.com/en/business/article/third-party-and-dynamic-tracking" target="_blank">Third-party and dynamic tracking</a>.
